\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00528}00528\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Widgets:\ Drag\ Sliders}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00529}00529\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ CTRL+Click\ on\ any\ drag\ box\ to\ turn\ them\ into\ an\ input\ box.\ Manually\ input\ values\ aren't\ clamped\ by\ default\ and\ can\ go\ off-\/bounds.\ Use\ ImGuiSliderFlags\_AlwaysClamp\ to\ always\ clamp.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00530}00530\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ For\ all\ the\ Float2/Float3/Float4/Int2/Int3/Int4\ versions\ of\ every\ function,\ note\ that\ a\ 'float\ v[X]'\ function\ argument\ is\ the\ same\ as\ 'float*\ v',}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00531}00531\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ the\ array\ syntax\ is\ just\ a\ way\ to\ document\ the\ number\ of\ elements\ that\ are\ expected\ to\ be\ accessible.\ You\ can\ pass\ address\ of\ your\ first\ element\ out\ of\ a\ contiguous\ set,\ e.g.\ \&myvector.x}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00532}00532\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Adjust\ format\ string\ to\ decorate\ the\ value\ with\ a\ prefix,\ a\ suffix,\ or\ adapt\ the\ editing\ and\ display\ precision\ e.g.\ "{}\%.3f"{}\ -\/>\ 1.234;\ "{}\%5.2f\ secs"{}\ -\/>\ 01.23\ secs;\ "{}Biscuit:\ \%.0f"{}\ -\/>\ Biscuit:\ 1;\ etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00533}00533\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Format\ string\ may\ also\ be\ set\ to\ NULL\ or\ use\ the\ default\ format\ ("{}\%f"{}\ or\ "{}\%d"{}).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00534}00534\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Speed\ are\ per-\/pixel\ of\ mouse\ movement\ (v\_speed=0.2f:\ mouse\ needs\ to\ move\ by\ 5\ pixels\ to\ increase\ value\ by\ 1).\ For\ gamepad/keyboard\ navigation,\ minimum\ speed\ is\ Max(v\_speed,\ minimum\_step\_at\_given\_precision).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00535}00535\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Use\ v\_min\ <\ v\_max\ to\ clamp\ edits\ to\ given\ limits.\ Note\ that\ CTRL+Click\ manual\ input\ can\ override\ those\ limits\ if\ ImGuiSliderFlags\_AlwaysClamp\ is\ not\ used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00536}00536\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Use\ v\_max\ =\ FLT\_MAX\ /\ INT\_MAX\ etc\ to\ avoid\ clamping\ to\ a\ maximum,\ same\ with\ v\_min\ =\ -\/FLT\_MAX\ /\ INT\_MIN\ to\ avoid\ clamping\ to\ a\ minimum.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00537}00537\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ We\ use\ the\ same\ sets\ of\ flags\ for\ DragXXX()\ and\ SliderXXX()\ functions\ as\ the\ features\ are\ the\ same\ and\ it\ makes\ it\ easier\ to\ swap\ them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00538}00538\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Legacy:\ Pre-\/1.78\ there\ are\ DragXXX()\ function\ signatures\ that\ take\ a\ final\ `float\ power=1.0f'\ argument\ instead\ of\ the\ `ImGuiSliderFlags\ flags=0'\ argument.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01131}01131\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Columns\ sizing\ policy\ allowed:\ Stretch\ (default),\ Fixed/Auto.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01132}01132\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Fixed\ Columns\ (if\ any)\ will\ generally\ obtain\ their\ requested\ width\ (unless\ the\ table\ cannot\ fit\ them\ all).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01133}01133\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Stretch\ Columns\ will\ share\ the\ remaining\ width\ according\ to\ their\ respective\ weight.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01134}01134\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Mixed\ Fixed/Stretch\ columns\ is\ possible\ but\ has\ various\ side-\/effects\ on\ resizing\ behaviors.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01135}01135\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ The\ typical\ use\ of\ mixing\ sizing\ policies\ is:\ any\ number\ of\ LEADING\ Fixed\ columns,\ followed\ by\ one\ or\ two\ TRAILING\ Stretch\ columns.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01136}01136\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ (this\ is\ because\ the\ visible\ order\ of\ columns\ have\ subtle\ but\ necessary\ effects\ on\ how\ they\ react\ to\ manual\ resizing).}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01141}01141\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ When\ using\ auto-\/resizing\ (non-\/resizable)\ fixed\ columns,\ querying\ the\ content\ width\ to\ use\ item\ right-\/alignment\ e.g.\ SetNextItemWidth(-\/FLT\_MIN)\ doesn't\ make\ sense,\ would\ create\ a\ feedback\ loop.}}
